%This is the script used to calculate all the significant amplitdues of 
%motion for the six degrees of motion. 
  
clear all 
clc 
  
%name of the excel file to upload 
name={'Sensitivity_pre-tension_tail_seawater.xlsx'}        
%loads all the sheets from the named excel file 
[status,sheets]=xlsfinfo('Sensitivity_pre-tension_tail_seawater.xlsx')     
%the time step in which to start, if more than one specify for each case 
time_surge=[1200]                                       
time_sway=[1000] 
time_heave=[1000] 
time_roll=[1000] 
time_pitch=[1000] 
time_yaw=[1000] 
  
%if different time steps, write this instead of n in time(n) 
for n=1:numel(sheets); 
surge(n)=SurgeSignificant(name,sheets(n),time_surge)         
sway(n)=SwaySignificant(name,sheets(n),time_sway) 
heave(n)=HeaveSignificant(name,sheets(n),time_heave) 
roll(n)=RollSignificant(name,sheets(n),time_roll) 
pitch(n)=PitchSignificant(name,sheets(n),time_pitch) 
yaw(n)=YawSignificant(name,sheets(n),time_yaw) 
end 
 
%This script calculates the significant motion of amplitude for sway. An 
%identical sheet has been created for the remaining degrees of motion, they 
%are not included hereafter. 
  
% clear all, clc, close all 
==PAGE:270==
function [FinalSigSway]=SwaySignificant(name,sheet,timestart) %function to 
run all sway motions together 
eval(sprintf('num=xlsread(''%s'',''%s'')',name{1},sheet{1}))   
sway=num(:,3)  %to indicate that sway is the 3rd column in the excel file  
t=num(:,1)      %to inicate that time is the first column in the excel file 
tstart=timestart 
n=1 
while t(n)<tstart 
    n=n+1; 
end 
nstart=n; 
meanSway=mean(sway(nstart:numel(t)))  %finding the mean sway to create a new 
"zero" line 
i=1 
for n=nstart:numel(t)                   %number of upward zero crossings 
    if sway(n-1)<meanSway && sway(n)>=meanSway 
        nupc(i)=n; 
        i=i+1; 
    end 
end  
for n=1:numel(nupc)-1;                   
    Max(n)=max(sway(nupc(n):nupc(n+1))) 
    Min(n)=min(sway(nupc(n):nupc(n+1)))  
end 
%% 
SigSway=Max-Min                    %finding the sway amplitude 
NoSigSway=1:numel(SigSway) 
PropSorted=NoSigSway/numel(SigSway) 
i=1; 
while PropSorted(i)<0.66 
    i=i+1 
end  
SigSwaySort=sort(SigSway); 
FinalSigSway=mean(SigSwaySort(i:numel(SigSwaySort)))    %average of top 1/3 
of sway values 
 
%In this script the 20yr time series from the MIKE21 SW is converted into 
%surge motions and mooring line forces for the scenario with the 
%Polypropylene line and no wind. A similar script has been made for all the 
%other scenarios, but they are not included here after. 
  
clear all 
clc 
  
name={'B7 1996-2015.xlsx'} 
sheet={'Ark1'} 
Data=xlsread('B7 1996-2015.xlsx' ,'Ark1'); 
Hmo=Data(:,1); 
Tp=Data(:,2); 
Dir=Data(:,3); 
for i=1:numel(Hmo) 
if Hmo(i)>0.7 && Hmo(i)<1.3                    %Loop for Hmo 1m 
  if Tp(i)>9.5 && Tp(i)<10.5                     %Tp 10s 
         Surge(i)=0.0003*exp(0.0182*Dir(i)); 
         MLF(i)=21706*exp(0.0041*Dir(i)); 
==PAGE:271==
     elseif Tp(i)>2.5 && Tp(i)<3.5                 %Tp 3s 
         Surge(i)=0.0007*exp(0.0098*Dir(i)); 
         MLF(i)=31642*exp(0.0017*Dir(i)); 
     elseif Tp(i)>3.5 && Tp(i)<4.5                 %Tp 4s 
         Surge(i)=0.0007*exp(0.0103*Dir(i)); 
         MLF(i)=32205*exp(0.0018*Dir(i)); 
     elseif Tp(i)>4.5 && Tp(i)<5.5               %Tp 5s 
         Surge(i)=0.0003*exp(0.0144*Dir(i));  
         MLF(i)=34383*exp(0.0017*Dir(i)); 
     elseif Tp(i)>5.5 && Tp(i)<6.5             %Tp 6s   
         Surge(i)=0.0005*exp(0.0129*Dir(i)); 
         MLF(i)=34688*exp(0.0018*Dir(i)); 
     elseif Tp(i)>6.5 && Tp(i)<7.5                 %Tp 7s   
         Surge(i)=0.0013*exp(0.01*Dir(i));   
         MLF(i)=36010*exp(0.0018*Dir(i)); 
     elseif Tp(i)>7.5 && Tp(i)<8.5            %Tp 8s 
         Surge(i)=0.0047*exp(0.0057*Dir(i));  
         MLF(i)=54412*exp(0.0004*Dir(i)); 
     elseif Tp(i)>8.5 && Tp(i)<9.5            %Tp 9s 
         Surge(i)=0.0009*exp(0.0128*Dir(i)); 
         MLF(i)=34267*exp(0.0023*Dir(i)); 
     elseif Tp(i)>10.5 && Tp(i)<11.5           %Tp 11s 
         Surge(i)=0.0004*exp(0.0177*Dir(i));  
         MLF(i)=41885*exp(0.0018*Dir(i)); 
     elseif Tp(i)>11.5 && Tp(i)<12.5             %Tp 12s 
         Surge(i)=0.0004*exp(0.018*Dir(i));  
         MLF(i)=49425*exp(0.0015*Dir(i)); 
     elseif Tp(i)>12.5 && Tp(i)<13.5           %Tp 13s 
         Surge(i)=0.0008*exp(0.0158*Dir(i)); 
         MLF(i)=45215*exp(0.0018*Dir(i)); 
     elseif Tp(i)>13.5 && Tp(i)<14.5           %Tp 14s 
        Surge(i)=0.0016*exp(0.0139*Dir(i));  
        MLF(i)=46990*exp(0.0019*Dir(i));

        Surge(i)=0.0026*exp(0.0127*Dir(i)); 
        MLF(i)=48382*exp(0.0018*Dir(i)); 
     elseif Tp(i)>15.5 && Tp(i)<16.5            %Tp 16s 
         Surge(i)=0.0006*exp(0.0188*Dir(i));

            MLF(i)=29677*exp(0.0034*Dir(i));

        elseif Tp(i)>6.5 && Tp(i)<7.5            %Tp 7s

            Surge(i)=0.000009*exp(0.0291*Dir(i)); 
            MLF(i)=34751*exp(0.0019*Dir(i)); 
        elseif Tp(i)>7.5 && Tp(i)<8.5            %Tp 8s
